***преподнести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a> (9914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднести.html>поднести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prepodnestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to make a present
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнёс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>prepodnjós</b> jej knígu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>presented</b> a book to her. / He <b>presented</b> her with a book.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́вом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́де</a> что́-либо кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnestí</b> v gotóvom víde štó-libo komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hand something to somebody on a plate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюрприз.html>сюрпри́з</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnestí</b> sjurpríz komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give somebody a surprise</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to communicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятный.html>неприя́тную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnestí</b> neprijátnuju nóvostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to communicate/bring bad news</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Délo v tom, kak éto <b>prepodnestí</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's a matter of presentation.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***преподносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a> (18694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подносить.html>подноси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prepodnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to make a present
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподно́сит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>prepodnósit</b> jej knígu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>is presenting</b> a book to her. / He <b>is presenting</b> her with a book.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́вом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́де</a> что́-либо кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnosítʹ</b> v gotóvom víde štó-libo komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hand something to somebody on a plate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюрприз.html>сюрпри́з</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnosítʹ</b> sjurpríz komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give somebody a surprise</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to communicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преподносить.html>преподноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятный.html>неприя́тную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepodnosítʹ</b> neprijátnuju nóvostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to communicate/bring bad news</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***препона.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́на</a> (31703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣпона</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prěpona</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пинать.html>пина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pinátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to kick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prepóna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obstacle, hindrance, impediment
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препятствие.html>препя́тствие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prepjátstvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:препона.html>препо́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stávitʹ <b>prepón</b> dlja rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put <b>obstacles</b> to work (ie, to hinder work)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:препятствовать.html>препя́тствовать</a> (9079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:препятствовать.html>препя́тствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prepjátstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспрепятствовать.html>воспрепя́тствовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hinder, to prevent, to prohibit, to impede, to put obstacles
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:препятствовать.html>препя́тствовать</a></b> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prepjátstvovatʹ</b> komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hinder someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прервать.html>прерва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prervátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прерывать.html>прерыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt, to break off, to sever, to discontinue, to cut short</li></ol>

***прерывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прерывать.html>прерыва́ть</a> (7672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прерывать.html>прерыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прервать.html>прерва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt, to break off, to sever, to discontinue</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пресекать.html>пресека́ть</a> (18546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пресе́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">presék-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресекать.html>пресека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">presekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресечь.html>пресе́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suppress, to stop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресекать.html>пресека́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">presekátʹ v kórne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nip in the bud</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***преследовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преследовать.html>пресле́довать</a> (4245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преследовать.html>пресле́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preslédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pursue, to chase</li>
<li>to persecute</li>
<li>to torment, to victimize</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prosecute</li>
<li>to strive (for); to pursue</li>
<li>to haunt</li></ol>
